>9e01	0c				    .byte   12              ; f -> FF (ASCII value 12)
>9e02	00 00 00 00 00			    .byte   0,0,0,0,0       ; g,h,i,j,k
>9e07	0a				    .byte   10              ; l -> LF (ASCII value 10)
>9e08	8d				    .byte   13+128          ; m -> CR/LF pair (ASCII values 13, 10)
>9e09	0a				    .byte   10              ; n behaves like l --> lf
>9e0a	00 00				    .byte   0,0             ; o,p
>9e0c	22				    .byte   34              ; q -> Double quote (ASCII value 34)
>9e0d	0d				    .byte   13              ; r ->  CR (ASCII value 13)
>9e0e	00				    .byte   0               ; s
>9e0f	09				    .byte   9               ; t -> Horizontal TAB (ASCII value 9)
>9e10	00				    .byte   0               ; u
>9e11	0b				    .byte   11              ; v -> Vertical TAB (ASCII value 11)
>9e12	00 00 00			    .byte   0,0,0           ; w,x,y   (x is a special case later)
